After a couple of moths, she didnâ€™t need the wheelchair anymore. She was running around my house again playing with her brothers. I'm all for the dog being provided the specialized wheelchair, so it can run and play. However it's disabled status does not grant it special rights to be off-leash. It could easily knock down a toddler and injure the child before the owner could reach the dog and restrain it. That's precisely why we have leash laws for all animals in public spaces. Fix this immediately so your dog doesn't injure someone or worse, and so your pet doesn't run into the street and be crushed to death by a motor vehicle.  As someone who is totally disabled, I have a clear understanding of why all disabled persons must abide by the laws and not try to  openly violate multiple laws every time we go somewhere. Driving a vehicle of any kind is an inherently dangerous activity for the driver, the passengers, as well as everyone on the road, crossing the road, walking beside the road either on the shoulder or a sidewalk. Disabled humans beings must therefore be extra vigilant when we are driving any kind of vehicle.   There are no laws regarding operating a motor vehicle, which only apply to disabled people or that apply only to those who are fully-abled.  Please be courteous and always ensure that your pets are always in compliance with all laws no matter where you are outside of your own property boundaries and also be hyper vigilant while operating any type of motor vehicle [including scooters, e bikes, e motorcycles, etc],so as to be doing everything in your power to prevent accidents as much as possible.  Thank you!
